Changshu: Source of Deposits in the General Affairs Office

Zhu Xingliang, the county accounting director, recently found a passbook in the general affairs office of the county government, with deposits of more than 18,000 yuan. Suspecting that it was suspicious, he seized the money and submitted it to the province for instructions. The source of this money has now been clarified as a special fund for the construction of county government warehouses. After this money was approved by the provincial department, the general affairs office of the county government immediately withdrew it from the fund management office, but did not deposit it into the treasury, and privately deposited the money into the bank, intending to obtain interest. Unified Price Increase in the Coal Industry

Now that it is winter, coal sales have increased sharply. The local coal industry has recently uniformly increased prices due to a lack of sources and low inventory starting from the 11th. They have also stopped charging accounts and are trading in cash only. The highest grade white coal for stoves is sold at 34 yuan per ton, and bituminous coal is sold at 22 yuan per ton.

Kunshan: Quartermaster Escapes with Funds, Burdening Guarantor

Li Zuolin, the quartermaster of the 9th Battalion of the Security Brigade stationed in Kunshan, suddenly escaped with more than 3,000 yuan of public funds some days ago. The authorities immediately detained Li's wife, Cai, and Miao Jinzian, a waitress at the Wenming Garden. After interrogation, they were released on bail. Suzhou: Construction of Roads in Xiangcheng Township

Qin Xigui, the district chief of Xiangcheng Township in Wu County, initiated the construction of roads because of the inconvenient transportation in the township and the frequent incursions of bandits, which is adjacent to Cheng Lake, in order to facilitate transportation. The road starts from Xiangcheng Town, passes through Taiping Town to reach the Suchang Highway. The entire road is more than ten li long, and the road surface is three meters wide. The earthwork project has already been completed, but bridges and culverts have not been built due to funding constraints. The Wu County Construction Bureau has sent special personnel to survey and is about to start building bridges. It is expected to be completed in two months.

Training of Commercial Organizations

Wu County has decided to start the training of people's organizations with commercial organizations first. After the commercial organizations are trained, the freelance professional organizations will be trained. The commercial organizations were originally scheduled to start on the 7th, but were postponed due to the lack of hired instructors. It has now been decided to form teams on the 13th, and hold an opening ceremony at Zhongshan Hall on the morning of the 14th, and start training on the same day. The training will last for one month. Due to the large number of people, it will be held in two phases. The first phase has a total of 501 people. All members of the executive and supervisory committees of the various trade associations must be trained, but those who have received self-government training can be exempted from training. The courses are divided into academic courses and technical courses, each lasting two hours. All uniforms are to be provided by the individuals themselves.

Clerk Sentenced for Smoking Opium

Zhu Xiongwu, a former clerk of the Civil Court of the Jiangsu High Court, was accused of smoking opium as a public official. He was sentenced to two years and six months in prison by the Wu County Government. The Jiangsu Provincial Government then ordered the county to retry the case. After the Wu County official retried the case, the verdict was issued yesterday. Zhu Xiongwu was given a reduced sentence of one year and six months in prison. The sentence will be carried out once it is approved.

Testing of Women's First Aid Class

The Women's First Aid Class founded by the Wu County Women's Association, with more than 100 students, has now completed its training period. The test will be held at Zhongshan Hall at 2:00 p.m. on the 12th. If the test is passed, certificates will be issued. The second phase may be postponed.

Wuxi: Strict Enforcement of Grain Storage Control

In order to prepare for grain storage and regulate people's food, the Resources Committee has strictly enforced grain storage control. All local grain storage, whether owned by the government or public by local organizations, may not be used without the approval of the provincial government. The provincial government has sent committee member Zhang Zhongyu to inspect Wuxi, Wu County, Wujiang and other three counties to assess the situation. The counties have been ordered to complete all procedures before the 15th of this month. After receiving the order, Long County magistrate of this county yesterday ordered the district chiefs to report the number of grain stored in this county within three days of receiving the document, in order to compile and forward it.

Active Grain Market

The local grain market has been quite active recently. Sailing ships are connected in the ponds and rivers around Beichang Sanliqiao, transporting rice up and down, and the situation is very tense. Next to the railway station, there are also piles of grain waiting for transportation by train. All rice mills on Jiangjianshang are working day and night to mill rice for sale at good prices. According to people in the rice industry yesterday, there are two reasons for the activity in the rice market: (1) The number of rice merchants coming to Xik to buy grain this year is more than in previous years, with some coming from as far as Xi'an and Tianjin, and some coming from counties such as Nantong, Haimen, Qidong, and Nanhui. (2) In recent years, agricultural warehouses have been established everywhere, so they are buying rice and grain for storage in preparation for famine relief. Therefore, the rice market is strong and there is no hope of decline. The prosperity of the rice shops is the greatest it has been in more than ten years.

Changzhou: Robbery and Injury in Lushu Township

Wu Yuansheng, a resident of Lushu Township in the third district of Wu County, is from a well-to-do family and has long been coveted by bandits. In the late hours of the 8th of this month, armed bandits suddenly broke down the door and entered his house to search and rob. The owner, Wu Yuansheng, woke up in his sleep and was unable to escape. He was grabbed, bound, and beaten by the bandits, suffering serious injuries. The bandits searched for a long time. Because the wind outside was urgent, they took the stolen goods and howled away. After checking, they found that they had been robbed of field deeds, clothes, and copper and tinware, suffering heavy losses. The district chief of the district, Zhu Tianying, reported the matter. Yesterday, he specially submitted the report to the county government, requesting strict arrest of the stolen goods and bandits for investigation and handling. It is also heard that Wu Yuansheng's family had previously been searched by bandits Zhong Koulin and others who have been executed, and a child was taken away.

Wu Huaiqin, the captain of the Shazhou Bridgehead Street Justice and Brave Ding Team in the third district, reported to the Yangku Public Security Third Branch that it was difficult to collect monthly donations, and detained Deng Ronggen, Fang Yunhua and other three merchants, arousing great public anger among more than 120 merchants in the town. The day before yesterday, they jointly went on strike, unanimously supporting them, and demanded the release from the branch. The situation may escalate.

Nantong: Verdict on Arson Case Due to Unrequited Love

Bao Ling, a well-known socialite in Tongcheng, once cohabited with Chen Zhensheng, the owner of the Sanyang Food Store, but recently suddenly broke up. After Chen Zhensheng's unrequited love, he attempted to extort money but failed and set fire to her house. The Public Security Bureau arrested him and sent him to the court. On the 10th, the criminal court concluded the trial. Chen Zhensheng was sentenced to twelve years in prison for extortion and arson.

Gaoyou: Soybean Oil Prices Soar

Soybean oil is a daily necessity. Recently, due to the shortage of raw materials and large-scale purchases by a certain country, the price of soybean oil has soared. On the 8th of this month, it was sold for 23.2 yuan per load, which is more than 4 yuan higher than before, and there is still a tendency for prices to continue to rise.

Zhenjiang: Thoroughly Reorganize Land Tax

The amount of arrears of old land tax in various counties of Jiangsu Province over the years is very large. Although the Finance Department has repeatedly decided to clear it up, the people are accustomed to the accumulated habits and it is difficult to thoroughly do so. Recently, the department revised the liquidation methods and submitted them to the provincial government meeting for approval. It is heard that the amount of land tax arrears in the counties from the 16th year of the Republic of China to the end of June this year, only the provincial regular tax item, reached more than 10 million yuan.

Yangzhou: Rice Shops Change to Pawnshops for Warehousing

The rice market outside Bianyimen in Yangzhou has always absorbed rice from the lower reaches of the river and transported it to various ports outside the Yangtze River, which is the main business. This year, due to the cheap rice in the south, the rice from the lower reaches is transported to the upper reaches for sale, resulting in a shortage of rice and the rice market is almost in a steep decline. Recently, there have been five companies that have announced their closure, and many more are on the verge of collapse. However, it is heard that Fucheng and Yulong have changed their operations to pawnshops due to the current situation. All rice and wheat transported are absorbed, valued at ten yuan and pledged for eight yuan. They charge storage rent and interest, and the business is still good. They have already stockpiled more than 40,000 stones. General speculators regard it as a stock exchange, receiving goods, mortgaging goods, and turning around busily, resulting in the rice price on the 9th and 10th increasing by about one yuan per stone. People in the industry said that during the winter when the water dries up and the green seedlings do not connect next spring, it will be possible to obtain special benefits by hoarding rice. Therefore, rice shops with insufficient general economies are even more affected.

Large Number of Famine Victims Arrive in Yangzhou

On the night of the 9th, 186 famine victims from Anhua, Hunan, suddenly arrived in Kongjia kiln, Duntou Township, in the fourth district of Jiangdu. The township head, Hu Derong, immediately reported to the fourth district office. The district chief, Liu Zhaorong, ordered township officials Gao Xiang and others to be responsible for expelling them. They have already left the border overnight. It is heard that they are begging along the way and maintaining order, without causing any disturbance.

Qingjiang: Accelerating the Dredging of Huai River, Working Overtime

The earthwork for dredging the Huai River assigned to Huai'an, Huaiyin, Lianshui, and Siyang counties has completed more than 80% so far, but accumulated sections are inevitable. The governments of the four counties have received orders from the province to increase labor and work overtime, in order to release water on New Year's Day of the 26th year without error. Among the four counties, Huai'an has the most unfinished earthwork, amounting to 2 million cubic meters. Therefore, the quota for additional labor in the county is also higher than in other counties, totaling 120,000 people. Zhang Guoqiong, the supervising officer sent by the provincial government, is stationed in the county to urge the work. The other three counties, Huaiyin, Lianshui, and Siyang, have half the number of additional labor as Huai'an, with Lianshui and Siyang having half the number of Huaiyin. In short, in order to avoid delays, the counties are adding night shifts to speed up the removal of earth in addition to the day shifts, so there is no difference.

Bengbu: Sheng Enyi Inspects Various Places

Sheng Enyi, director of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Unified Tax Bureau, recently set off on a visit to all subordinate agencies to inspect the actual situation of manufacturers in order to improve administrative efficiency. He arrived in Bengbu from Nanjing on the 10th. It is heard that he will go to Anqing, Wuhu, and other places to continue his inspection in the coming days.

Jiashan: Tense Kiln Work

In order to increase the service knowledge of the staff, the kiln management office of this county has specially hired experts as lecturers, and held a lecture hall for three days in the auditorium of the county government starting on the 10th. The topics are the management, manufacturing, production and sales, organization of the kiln industry, and various special topics. A research committee was also organized, with the appointment of Shen Jiren and other thirteen people as members, and Xue Zheshen was elected as the standing committee member to engage in research. Seven kiln districts were also divided, and a kiln cooperative was organized in each district, with Guan Mingfu, Zhu Lejun and other twenty-nine people engaged in preparation.

Jiaxing: Urging Commercial Registration

Since the commercial registration of Jiaxing has been planned and assisted by the County Chamber of Commerce, most of them have been fulfilled. A small number of merchants still hold a wait-and-see attitude, although the County Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly decided to send personnel to persuade them. Now, in order to complete the general registration within the time limit, the county government has sent many policemen to supervise the various sections and fill out the forms within a limited time. If the deadline is exceeded, the police will be ordered to detain and punish them. Yesterday, Xiangyuan and other numbers were detained and fined.

Xiaoshan: Winter Joint Land and Water Defense

Xiaoshan organized winter defense and followed the order of the Commissioner's Office of the Third District, strictly preventing vagrant soldiers and hooligans from causing accidents and disturbances. Therefore, the joint military and police office has been searching for vagrant soldiers and unemployed hooligans in urban and rural areas for days. As for the inland river defense along the Xiaoshan Xiaojiang Qianjiang area, it is the responsibility of the water public security team to deploy.

Educational News

Jiangsu Province Education Association: Decision to Promote Compulsory Education Plan; Outline for the 26th Year Drafted; Each County to Establish at Least Twenty School Classes

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, considering it imperative to formulate a plan for promoting compulsory education in the 26th year, and recognizing that each county must raise additional funding to ensure smooth implementation, convened a meeting of the Provincial Compulsory Education Committee a few days ago. The following is the drafted outline for the compulsory education plan for the 26th year: (1) All compulsory education classes established in counties and cities during the 24th and 25th years shall continue to operate in the 26th year. (2) The number of new compulsory education classes to be added in each county and city in the 26th year shall be determined based on local financial resources and environmental needs, but the principle is to establish at least twenty classes. In special circumstances, adjustments may be made with approval. (3) The funding for compulsory education in each county and city in the 26th year shall primarily be self-raised. The provincial subsidy will be based on local self-raised funds, divided into four categories: two-thirds, one-half, one-third, and one-quarter. The annual class fee shall not exceed 300 yuan as the maximum standard. (4) New compulsory education classes shall primarily operate as two-part short-term elementary schools. Ordinary classes shall not be established unless absolutely necessary. (5) Compulsory education teachers shall continue to be recruited primarily from normal school graduates. Short-term compulsory education teacher training classes will also be organized by the provincial normal schools and rural normal schools in each normal school district. (6) In the 26th year, actively supervise the improvement of private schools, selectively providing subsidies to the best. (7) Compulsory education classes in the provincial capital will continue to be promoted according to the previous year's plan.

Seventeen Counties Including Shanghai Hold Meeting of Scout Leaders; Request Ministry of Education to Include Cub Scout Training as Required Course in Elementary Schools

The joint meeting of scout leaders from seventeen counties including Shanghai was held last week at the Shanghai County Party Headquarters. Representatives from Shanghai, Songjiang, Jinshan, Nanhui, Chuansha, Baoshan, Qingpu, Taicang, Jiading, Kunshan, Chongming, Qidong, Haimen, and other counties, totaling more than 20 people, attended. Zhang Gongren and Chen Bangcai were specially dispatched by the Jiangsu Provincial Council to attend and provide guidance. Zhang Gongren was elected as chairman of the meeting. First, the chairman delivered the opening address, followed by Chen Bangcai reporting on the work of the Provincial Council over the past year. Then, the county council representatives gave their reports separately. After that, the motions were discussed: (1) A motion to request the Provincial Council to suggest to the General Association not to easily change the style of scout uniforms was passed. (2) A motion to request the Provincial Council to suggest to the General Association that scout registration be handled by the provincial councils starting from the 26th year was passed. (3) The expenses for each county to hold scout inspections and jamborees are very large. In addition to subsidies from the county party headquarters and education bureaus, they are often insufficient. It was resolved that the provincial government should order the county governments to provide appropriate subsidies to facilitate progress. The resolution was referred to the Provincial Council for processing. (4) A motion to request the Provincial Council to suggest to the General Association that experts should be quickly commissioned to edit special training materials for scouts to meet urgent needs was passed. (5) A motion to request the Provincial Council to suggest to the General Association that the qualification standards for the three levels of scout training and the qualification standards for both pre and post-period cub scout training should be re-established to ensure consistency was passed. (6) Although the funds of each county party headquarters have been slightly tightened, the subsidy fees for each county council should still be maintained. It was resolved that the Provincial Council should negotiate with the Provincial Party Headquarters. (7) A letter was sent to the Ministry of Education requesting that cub scout training be included as a required subject in elementary schools and that cub scout uniforms be stipulated as elementary school uniforms. The motion was passed.

Sports News

National Physical Education Implementation Measures: Central People's Training Department Promulgates to All Party Departments to Order Phased Implementation

(Central News Agency, Nanjing) The People's Training Department of the Central Party Headquarters, in order to promote national physical education, has formulated an implementation plan for national physical education guidance work and issued it to all levels of party departments for compliance and implementation. It is now necessary to formulate implementation measures for national physical education training based on the plan, stipulating a five-year plan for the implementation of national physical education training, to be implemented in phases and gradually. It has been submitted to the Central Standing Committee for record and promulgated to all levels of party departments for compliance and implementation. From now on, national physical education can be expected to progress steadily. The following excerpts from the measures are provided: (1) When party departments at all levels implement the national physical education guidance work implementation plan promulgated by the Central People's Training Department, they shall follow these measures, except where the plan has already stipulated otherwise.

Phased Implementation

(2) The implementation of national physical education training is divided into two phases: the first phase is tentatively set for two years, and the second phase is tentatively set for three years. The implementation work standards for each phase are as follows: First Phase: 1. Establish provincial, municipal, and county physical education associations in all provinces, cities, and counties. 2. Make the public aware of the importance of physical education and hygiene and generate interest. 3. Increase the number of sports venues and equipment. 4. Prepare training classes for physical education cadres. Second Phase: 1. Expand the organization of provincial, municipal, and county physical education associations and establish municipal district/neighborhood and county district/township physical education associations in each municipal district/neighborhood and county district/township. 2. Find ways to develop the public's habit of using physical education as entertainment. 3. Actively implement public physical education training and ensure that sports venues and equipment are sufficient for the use of most of the public.

Implementation Items

(3) The items for implementation in each phase are as follows: First Phase: A. Regarding investigation and design: 1. Investigate existing sports organizations and their structures. 2. Investigate the types of sports that the public prefers. 3. Investigate folk games. 4. Investigate the public's occupational life. 5. Investigate the public's leisure life. 6. Investigate existing sports venues and equipment. 7. Investigate suitable locations for the construction of sports venues. 8. Investigate physical education teachers and personnel capable of guiding work. 9. Investigate the physical education situation in various institutions and schools. 10. Investigate other physical education investigation matters related to the area. 11. Formulate various physical education laws, regulations, methods, and implementation outlines based on the conditions in each area. B. Regarding organization and training: 1. Organize provincial, municipal, and county physical education associations. 2. Adjust the organization of existing sports groups. 3. Urge people's organizations to organize physical education associations and join the local physical education association as group members. 4. Organize various sports competitions regularly. 5. Cooperate with health agencies to handle health matters and promulgate bans to eliminate bad habits that harm physical education. 6. Hold cadre training classes. C. Regarding publicity: 1. Draw physical education and hygiene posters and slogans and post them in major transportation routes and densely populated areas to attract public attention. 2. Set up physical education bulletin boards to publish physical education news, biographies of sports celebrities, and hygiene knowledge. 3. Convene the public to lecture on physical education knowledge. 4. Invite sports stars to perform. D. Regarding equipment: 1. Repair and increase the construction of sports venues and equipment. 2. Public agencies with 50 or more employees should try to build their own sports venues within the possible range. 3. Large factories and larger companies and shops should build their own sports venues with funds. Second Phase: A. Regarding investigation and design: 1. Continue the investigation and design items of the first phase. 2. Investigate the effectiveness of the first phase of implementation. B. Regarding organization and training: 1. Universally organize municipal district/neighborhood and county district/township physical education branches in each municipal district/neighborhood and county district/township, and widely solicit members. 2. Assist the public in organizing trade physical education associations to expand membership solicitation. 3. Continue to run physical education cadre training classes. 4. Conduct public physical fitness examinations. 5. Hold various joint sports competitions. 6. Hold sports tests. C. Regarding publicity: 1. Screen sports films and slides at any time. 2. Publish sports publications. 3. Invite sports experts to give lectures. 4. Continue to carry out the publicity work of the first phase. D. Regarding equipment: 1. Expand existing sports venues and increase their construction. 2. Increase the construction of sports venues in densely populated villages within the possible range.

Types of Sports

(4) The selection of sports should focus on strengthening the body and mind and cultivating national defense skills. Examples are as follows: (1) Track and field; (2) Ball games; (3) Chinese martial arts; (4) Swimming; (5) Equestrian archery; (6) Gymnastics; (7) Mechanical sports; (8) Folk games; (9) Various sports that are suitable for local customs, climates, and weather conditions. 5. Sports venues should be utilized as much as possible. All public and private clubs, physical education associations, public sports venues, school sports grounds, etc., should be fully utilized or the local hillsides, ditches, ponds, swamps, forests, lawns, temples, etc., should be converted into sports venues and children's playgrounds. 6. The time for sports should be based on the principle of not hindering the public's business. The provincial, municipal, and county physical education associations may decide and announce them according to the circumstances. 7. Physical education personnel in each province and city should go to various areas to guide local school physical education teachers, school sports stars, and military police and civilians who have physical education training may be hired as voluntary instructors at any time. 8. If there are any matters not covered in these measures, the Central People's Training Department shall submit them to the Central Standing Committee for approval and amendment. 9. These measures shall be implemented after being submitted to the Central Standing Committee for record and promulgated by the Central People's Training Department.

Finance: Shorts Increase Positions; Gold Price First Firm, Then Turns Flat

Although pure gold in Yu City rose yesterday, the market once rose, but because shorts took advantage of the high price to increase their positions, it soon fell back. Spot firms took advantage of the low price to limit purchases, and finally settled. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets, both England and the United States rose, and the forward silver price spread in Montede reduced by about three and a half licks. The exchange rate opened flat and closed higher. London raw gold rose by three and a half pence. The Central Bank's pegging was announced, both England and the United States were flat. The Customs gold unit rose by four cents. The standard gold price was listed at 255 yuan and one dime. The over-the-counter pre-market transaction opened, and it rose to about 55 yuan and a half. Sugar Market: Over a Thousand Pieces of Green Slab Sugar from Shek Mun Anticipated for Exchange

Yesterday, the sugar market saw little change. The guild's price for existing stock of No. 24 coarse white sugar was 21.55 yuan, while re-exported goods were at 6.125 yuan. Dong Bai Nos. 4 and 8 remained at their original prices, but No. 9 decreased slightly by 0.05 yuan. Existing stock of YRO marked sugar was 21 yuan, and re-exported goods were at 5.9 yuan. Mian Bai No. 1 from the local factory, Zhen Ji, was 20.4 yuan, and Nos. 2, 3, 4, and 5 followed suit. The price board listed over a thousand pieces of green slab sugar from Shek Mun, to be delivered in one week, at a price of 10.05 yuan to 10.45 yuan.

The joint venture company yesterday held its third tender for Cantonese sugar this week, with a total fixed quota of 10,789 bags. The bid prices remained as before. 770 bags of coarse white sugar from the Shunde factory, Five Rams brand, were sold at 21.3 yuan; 100 bags from the City New Factory were sold at 21.1 yuan; 15 bags from Shantou were sold at 20.9 yuan; and another 50 bags were sold at 20.7 yuan, for a total of 935 bags sold.

Dried Goods: Dried Longan Slightly Dropping by One or Two Yuan

The sales of dried longan have recently slowed down, and there have been no new shipments of high-quality goods. After investigating, over a hundred pieces have arrived, but have not yet been put on the market. It is rumored that some are eager to sell off small quantities, leading to a slight decrease of one or two yuan in the black market. This has already happened. As for Hainan goods, the stock is relatively abundant, but due to cost considerations, there is little hope of a significant price drop. The future market will depend on sales picking up before bulk transactions can occur.

Shanghai Cultural Circles: Banquet for Tian Bo Lie Last Night; Tian Visited Mayor Wu and Attended a Welcome Banquet; Lecture at the YMCA This Afternoon at 4 PM

Tian Bo Lie, President of the International Historical Society and Professor at Cambridge University, a world-renowned historian, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday during his world tour and is staying at the International Hotel. At 11:00 AM yesterday, accompanied by Kang Xuan Yi, he went to the city center to visit Mayor Wu Tiecheng. The Mayor received him in the reception room on the third floor, expressing deep admiration for this scholar of the era and inviting him to stay in Shanghai for a few more days. Afterwards, he visited the construction in the city center. At noon, the Mayor hosted a banquet at his private residence on Haige Road to welcome Mr. Tian, inviting Chen Guangfu, Yang Guangxing, Guo Bingwen, Cai Zengji, and Kang Xuanyi, among others, to accompany. At 5:30 PM, he went to the China Funeral Home to pay respects to Huang Fu. At 7:00 PM, the International Affairs Research Society, the Universal Student Association, the Sino-Foreign Cultural Association, the Professor Writers Association, and the Peking University Alumni Association, among other groups, hosted a welcome banquet for Mr. Tian at the YMCA at the Eight Immortals Bridge. Attendees included Mayor Wu (represented by Pan Gongzhan), Cui Wei Wu, Zhang Shouyong, Li Dachao, Yan Fuqing, Li Ximou, Jiang Jianbai, Kang Xuanyi, Zhu Shaoping, Li Guansan, Du Gangbai, Chen Hongfan, Chen Derong, Ding Zheming, Yu Liang, Cui Xiaocen, Deng Qingshan, He Zhenya, Wang Chuntao, Bao Tianxiao, and Mr. and Mrs. Tian Bo Lie, among others, totaling several dozen people. First, Jiang Jianbai delivered a welcome speech on behalf of everyone, translated by Dai Baozhao, stating that Mr. Tian Bo Lie is a world-renowned historical expert, and China is an ancient country with a long history of civilization, so there is a real need for research methods on history. Mr. Tian Bo Lie's visit to China will surely provide people with practical instructions, so that the research methods of Chinese and foreign history can be integrated into one. Therefore, I represent everyone to express sincere welcome. Then, Mayor Wu delivered a speech on behalf of Director Pan, briefly saying that it is of profound significance that today the cultural groups of this city welcome Mr. Tian Bo Lie. Everyone knows that Mr. Tian has many extremely valuable works, such as the Paris Peace Conference, Historical Materials of the European War, and England and the Near East, etc. Not only are the materials collected rich and authentic, but they have also greatly contributed to the communication of human civilization and the promotion of peace. This time, Mr. Tian Bo Lie's visit to the Far East for exploration and investigation will surely make the actual situation in the Far East clear to the world, which will also have a great relationship with world peace. The International Historical Society organized by Mr. Tian Bo Lie has already been joined by forty-two countries, and Japan has recently joined. We want to take this opportunity to arouse the attention of domestic cultural circles to join the association. The cultural circles in the capital and Peiping have already expressed their intention to join, and it is hoped that the cultural circles in this city will also make the same expression. This should be welcome news to Mr. Tian Bo Lie, and I hope that after the annual meeting is held in Switzerland in 1938, the annual meeting in 1940 can be held in China. We will sincerely welcome Mr. Tian Bo Lie and all members. Finally, I hope that Mr. Tian Bo Lie can visit universities in China, such as Dewey's, and I wish Mr. and Mrs. Tian good health. Then, Mr. Tian Bo Lie gave a speech, briefly saying, I am very grateful for the welcome from the cultural circles in your place today. I have been to several places since I came here. What impressed me the most is that everything in your country shows vitality. Whether in cultural, military, or political circles, there are extremely many young people. This is clear evidence, so I predict that China will have a bright future. The reason why I came to your country this time is that due to time constraints, I have not yet prepared for writing. What I hope for from the cultural circles of your country is that in the future they can join the International Historical Society, because this association has already been joined by more than 40 countries, which will enable the cultural circles of China to communicate with the cultural circles of various countries in the future. For example, Mr. Hu Shih in the cultural circles of your country has a very good reputation in the world. I hope that in the future, he can work with the cultural circles of your country to participate in international cultural work, so as to enhance the purpose of international cultural undertakings. Mr. Tian is scheduled to give a public lecture at the YMCA at Eight Immortals Bridge at 4:30 PM today, with the topic being "International Situation and Internationalism," which will surely be a grand occasion.

[Image Caption] Tian Bo Lie (center) and the banquet attendees (International Press Photo)

The Nonagenarian Departs for Beijing This Morning

Mr. Ma Xiangbo, the nonagenarian, has been residing in Shanghai for a long time. Recently, due to the persuasion of Mr. Feng Yuxiang, Yu Youren and others, it has been decided that this morning (the 12th), he will take a special train prepared by the Ministry of Railways to Beijing for a short stay, and has selected No. 12 Dafang Lane in front of the Drum Tower in the capital as his residence. In addition to his daughter-in-law, Madam Ma Qiu Renwo, his granddaughter, Miss Ma Yuzhang, and his grand-nephew, Mr. Ma Fengzhang, those accompanying him include President Yu Youren and many members of the Supervisory Yuan. His family members are afraid that the elderly man will be tired from the journey, so they specially instructed his medical consultant, Mr. Li Quanjing, to accompany and protect him.

[Image Caption] The nonagenarian and his medical consultant

Song Ziwen to Arrive Tomorrow

Song Ziwen, a member of the Standing Committee of the National Economic Council, completed his inspection tour to the south yesterday. He and Bei Songsun and Chen Kangzhai are on their way back north on the Japanese Empress, a Chang Yu Company ship, and are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 13th. Also on the same ship are Liu Weichi, Director of the Construction Department of Guangdong Province, Liu Jiwen, a provincial committee member, and Zhang Huichang, the ambassador to Cuba, and others.

Zhu Jia Hua Flew to Shanghai Yesterday to Meet Huang Shao Hong to Discuss Handover

The newly appointed Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Zhu Jiahua, went to Xi'an to meet with President Chiang for instructions. After returning to Nanjing the day before yesterday, it is now known that Mr. Zhu took a China Aviation Corporation plane to Shanghai yesterday afternoon to meet with Huang Shaohong, the former Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, to discuss handover matters. After returning to Nanjing once again in the next few days, he will go to Hangzhou around the 18th to take office.

Xu Kan Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Xu Kan, the Permanent Vice Minister of Finance, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing by train at around 7:00 AM yesterday morning. After returning to his residence for a short rest, he went to the Central Bank to meet with Finance Minister Kong to ask for instructions on departmental affairs.

Inspector General of Customs, Meierhe, Going to Guangdong to Inspect Customs and Smuggling

Meierhe, the Inspector General of Customs of the Ministry of Finance, left Shanghai by ship the day before yesterday and went south to Guangdong. Meierhe's trip is to inspect the customs duties in Guangdong Province and the smuggling situation in South China. He plans to stay in Guangdong for two weeks and then return north to report the inspection process to the financial authorities so that he can reform and rectify.

Cai Zimin's Condition

Cai Jiemin, President of the National Central Research Institute, has been feeling unwell since the 28th of last month. Initially, he was diagnosed by Song Wusheng, a doctor at the institute. After a few days, Wu Xudan, a doctor from the Red Cross Hospital, and Xie Bi (Hibert), a French doctor, were invited for a consultation. Recently, Yan Fuqing, Dean of the National Shanghai Medical College, invited Yue Wenzhao, Director of Internal Medicine at the college, and Weng Zhilong, President of National Tongji University, invited Kastein, a professor at the university, to join the consultation. It is reported that because Mr. Cai is old and weak, his condition is deeply worrying. Deposited Palace Museum Artifacts, Second Batch Transported to Nanjing Yesterday, Totaling 4,817 Boxes

The artifacts from the Palace Museum stored in Shanghai were all transported to Nanjing and stored in the Central Antiquities Preservation Warehouse at Chaotian Palace in Nanjing after the warehouse was completed, with the approval of the Executive Yuan. The first batch of 3,151 boxes was transported to Nanjing on the evening of the 8th of this month. Yesterday, the second batch continued to be transported. The Executive Yuan's Ministry of Education specially appointed escorts, Shu Chushi and Ding Wenyuan, etc., to work with all the staff of the Shanghai Office of the Palace Museum to open the warehouse door at the storage warehouse on Tianzhu Church Street at 6:00 AM yesterday to start moving. The transport special train prepared by the Railway Bureau was still parked at the Macgregor Road station for loading. The transportation from the preparation warehouse to the Macgregor Road station was still handled by Moutai Foreign Company, and armed Chinese police officers sent by the French patrol room escorted the vehicle. Police officers were stationed and guarded around Tianzhu Church Street. At the Macgregor Road station, soldiers from the Garrison Headquarters and soldiers from the Security Regiment and railway police were on guard. The transportation started at 6:00 AM and ended at 5:00 PM, totaling 4,817 boxes marked with "Hu," "Shang," and "Gong." The types of artifacts transported included porcelain, jade, bronze, tin, calligraphy and painting, and various archives. The remaining artifacts stored in Shanghai will continue to be transported.

Shanghai Municipal Annals Hall Obtains: The Shanghai County Annals of the Hongzhi Era of the Ming Dynasty, The First Annals of Shanghai County, Missing for More Than 250 Years

The Shanghai Municipal Annals Hall has been dedicated to compiling and researching the historical facts of various departments in Shanghai, and has long been recognized internationally for its reputation. Its interviews and collection of works related to Shanghai are also highly praised by the people of the country. Recently, the hall obtained the Shanghai County Annals of the Hongzhi Era of the Ming Dynasty, which can be regarded as an unprecedented achievement. According to the Shanghai County Annals, there are a total of ten copies from the Ming Dynasty to the present. The first copy was compiled by Tang Jin in the seventeenth year of Hongzhi (1504). This record was not seen when the record was revised in the twenty-second year of Kangxi in the Qing Dynasty (1683). Since then, it has never been found during the revision of the record in various dynasties. The Shanghai Municipal Annals Hall has made great efforts to collect Shanghai records from past dynasties, and has paid more attention to the Hongzhi record, conducting interviews everywhere. It was learned that the Hongzhi record was still left in the Tianyi Pavilion in Ningbo. Overjoyed, it began negotiations with Tianyi Pavilion in the summer of the twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China to copy and print it. In the autumn of the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, the hall commissioned Xu Weixuan, a teacher at Ningbo Girls' High School, to directly negotiate with Mr. Feng Mengzhen of the Tianyi Pavilion Reconstruction Committee, and then obtained a photograph and transcription, and Mr. Xu carefully proofread it. As a result, the Shanghai County Annals of Hongzhi, which had been unseen for more than 250 years, was returned to its hometown. This is indeed a major contribution of the Shanghai Municipal Annals Hall to the city.

Lie Feng Silk Factory Increases Wages: Settlement Minutes Signed Yesterday, Stipulating Wage Rates for Sanmin Ni, etc.

Yi Zhong Pudong Factory: Labor Dispute Resolved, Settlement Minutes Signed Yesterday

After the workers of the Yi Zhong Fuzhi Porcelain Pudong Factory went on strike, the Party and government authorities advised them to resume work first. Regarding the request for improved treatment, the Bureau of Social Affairs called Zhang Heshang, a representative of the workers, and Zhou Qi, a representative of the capitalists, etc. to mediation at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. The two parties agreed and signed the settlement minutes, stipulating: (1) Starting from January next year, the factory shall, depending on their daily performance and diligence, moderately increase the wages of other workers, except for a few workers with poor work performance and new workers. (2) All workers who continue to work for a full month without interruption due to any reason shall be rewarded with one day of work. (3) Regardless of whether they are male or female workers, those who work on Sundays or night shifts shall be paid an additional 20% of their monthly wages.

The Ministry of Communications is Hosting the National Ship Registration and Promulgated Registration Rules Yesterday

The Ministry of Communications promulgated the Ship Industry Registration Rules yesterday to conduct national ship registration. The original text is explored as follows: Article 1: Anyone engaged in the ship industry must apply to the competent maritime administration agency in accordance with these rules and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for approval and registration, and may operate only after a license is issued. If it is a company organization, it must also register with the Ministry of Industry in accordance with the Company Law and its related regulations, and the same applies when it changes. Article 2: The applicant for the ship industry is as follows: (1) For public enterprises, the organizer shall submit a request or consult; (2) For people who operate solely or jointly, the investor shall submit a request; (3) For unlimited companies, all shareholders shall submit a request; (4) For limited liability companies, all shareholders with unlimited liability shall submit a request; (5) For joint-stock limited companies, all directors and supervisors shall submit a request; (6) For joint-stock limited liability companies, all shareholders with unlimited liability and all supervisors shall submit a request; (7) For people and public enterprises jointly operating, it shall be handled in accordance with the regulations for joint operation. Article 3: When applying for registration of the ship industry, the following matters should be stated: (1) Company or firm name; (2) Articles of Association; (3) Location of the headquarters and branches; (4) Business routes (with illustrations); (5) Business plan (such as purchasing several ships, operating on a scheduled or unscheduled basis, or a combination of scheduled and unscheduled, and building docks, etc.); (6) List of shareholders (or investment institutions); (7) Names, ages, native places, and addresses of the founders and managers; (8) General estimate of start-up costs and general estimate of business revenue and expenditure, etc.; (9) Other relevant matters. The above books and pictures shall be made in duplicate, and shall be kept and transferred by the competent maritime administration agency. Article 4: After the ship industry's business routes and operations on a scheduled or unscheduled basis, or a combination of scheduled and unscheduled, have been approved and registered and a license has been issued, they shall not be changed without applying for review. Article 5: When applying for registration of the ship industry, in addition to paying a stamp duty of two yuan, a registration fee shall be paid in accordance with the following regulations: 10 yuan for those below 10,000 yuan, 20 yuan for those below 300,000 yuan, 30 yuan for those below 500,000 yuan, 40 yuan for those below 800,000 yuan, 50 yuan for those below 1 million yuan, and for those exceeding 1 million yuan, an additional 50 yuan shall be charged for every 1 million yuan. If the amount is less than 1 million yuan, it shall be calculated as 1 million yuan. When companies and firms established before the implementation of these rules apply for registration, their registration fees shall be reduced by one-third. The registration fee for public ship industries shall be reduced by one-half. Article 6: When the ship industry changes its name or organization, it shall apply to the competent maritime administration agency and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for approval to reissue the license. Article 7: If any of the following circumstances occur in the ship industry, it shall first apply to the competent maritime administration agency and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for approval: (1) Increase or decrease capital; (2) Issue corporate bonds; (3) Increase, decrease or change routes. Article 8: When the ship industry is dissolved, the original license shall be returned for cancellation. Article 9: If the result of increasing capital causes the original registration fee to be insufficient for the amount prescribed in Article 5, it shall be paid in full. Article 10: When the ship industry suspends business, it shall report to the competent maritime administration agency and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for record. If business is suspended for more than six months, the license shall be revoked, but this shall not apply to cases caused by natural disasters or other force majeure. Article 11: Ship companies and firms that have been established before the promulgation and implementation of these rules shall apply for registration within six months from the date of implementation of these rules. Article 12: After the ship industry registration is approved, it shall commence business within one year. If it cannot be opened as scheduled due to special circumstances, it shall apply to the competent maritime administration agency and submit it to the Ministry of Communications for approval to extend the period. Otherwise, the department shall revoke its registration. The aforementioned extension shall be limited to one time and shall not exceed one year. Article 13: These rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

City General Labor Union Denies Participating in Asian Labor Conference

The Dagong News Agency reports that a previous news report from the Allied News Agency claimed that amidst the bleak Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations, the Shanghai General Labor Union of the Chinese labor community would send representatives in April of next year to hold an Asian Labor Conference with the Japanese labor community to shake hands, etc. A reporter from the Dagong News Agency, in order to understand the truth, specifically visited Mr. Zhu Xuefan, the chairman of the Shanghai General Labor Union yesterday. According to his reply, the Asian Labor Conference was initiated and convened by the Japanese labor community. This year, they sent a letter to the China branch of the International Labor Bureau, which forwarded it to our union, asking us to send representatives to participate in the second conference to be held in Tokyo in April of next year, and attached the union's constitution. After reviewing the articles, the aim was to avoid war, establish international peace, and resist imperialism and capitalism. After the union submitted it for discussion, everyone agreed that because of the rampant imperialism, China's industry and commerce were collapsing, the rural areas were bankrupt, unemployment was increasing frequently, and the workers' suffering was profound. Moreover, due to Japan's continuous aggression, the national crisis was imminent. Of course, we agreed with the union's proposal to maintain peace. However, what the Japanese government and people have shown in fact is the opposite. They believe that it is impossible to participate before Japan changes its aggressive policies. The union should send a letter to the Japanese Labor Union based on this point, stating its wishes, and hoping that the Japanese labor community will urge the military authorities to reflect. As for the Allied News Agency's telegram that the union has replied to participate and shake hands with the Japanese labor community, this is not true.

Silk Factories Run Out of Raw Materials, Liyuan and Thirteen Other Factories Suspend Operations

After the price of Chinese silk in the European and American markets fell, all 48 silk factories operating in Shanghai suspended operations one after another due to running out of raw materials. As of yesterday, the factories that suspended operations included Hengtai, Zhenxiang, Dingchang, Yicheng, Shaoxing, Hongtai, Fuchang No. 2, Yutai, Yufeng, Yuanxing, Yuanji, China, and Liyuan, totaling thirteen factories. Factories such as Dongxiang and Yufeng have already run out of raw materials and will suspend operations immediately. As for the remaining factories that are still operating, such as Jiyu, it is expected that they will also suspend operations before the end of January.

The Dagong News Agency reports that the European and American silk markets have been fluctuating recently. In October, they rose sharply, and each dan of Shanghai white silk could be sold for around 900 yuan. By last month, due to speculators taking the opportunity to act, the overseas markets all saw a decline. Each dan of Shanghai white silk fell by about 40 to 50 yuan. At the beginning of this month, it fell again. Currently, in the overseas market, each dan of Shanghai white silk is only sold for about 750 yuan, a sharp drop of more than 100 yuan compared to October. Moreover, sales are very sluggish, and the markets in the United States and France are at a standstill. The previous export volume was 55,077 bales, while the last export volume was only 38,961 bales, a decrease of about two-tenths. Moreover, because the end of the year is approaching and various industries will be settling accounts, it is difficult to expect improvement for the time being.

Autumn Cocoons Fail to Yield Good Harvest

The current Jiangzhe autumn cocoon harvest has failed to yield a good harvest and is not enough for the silk factories to use. Therefore, factories have continued to suspend operations in recent days. However, because this year's spring cocoon harvest was abundant, most cocoon merchants purchased a lot. Because the European and American silk markets were showing signs of improvement between September and October, they were hoarding and unwilling to sell easily. According to a survey by the silk industry, there are still 10,000 to 20,000 dan of cocoons stored in Shanghai foreign firms. If factories purchase from them, their prices are high. Based on the current silk market, it is not possible to make a profit. Therefore, silk factories are willing to suspend operations rather than continue production. Currently, 33 factories in the city are still operating, half of which still have spring cocoon reserves, which are enough to last until the end of the lunar year. The other factories will all suspend operations within days. It is feared that Shanghai silk factories will not be able to operate in the spring of next year.

Improving Sericulture

The Jiangzhe Provinces Sericulture Unification and Improvement Committee, because it was aware that few rural families raised silkworms last year, which was not enough for silk factories to reel, made every effort to promote the increase of rearing households in the spring of last year, and changed all native varieties to improved varieties. However, due to time constraints, some areas were not able to improve them, and because the mulberry leaves were not enough for the silkworms to eat, it was not possible to promote them universally. According to silk factory merchants, the authorities of Jiangzhe provinces, being aware that this year's silkworm cocoons are still not enough for reeling, are now working hard to promote them. For example, in Zhejiang Province, in counties such as Changxing, Wuxing, Wukang, Jiaxing, Haining, Haiyan, Yuqian, Fuyang, Xindeng, Shengxian, and Xinchang, they are guiding silkworm farmers to uniformly raise improved varieties next spring. In Jiangsu Province, places such as Suzhou, Wuxi, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, and Nanjing are also doing the same, and all miscellaneous varieties will be eliminated. Regarding mulberry trees, they have also guided rural farmers to actively cultivate them. Currently, in Jiangsu Province, only the Zhenjiang area has planted mulberry trees, which can yield about 40,000 dan of leaves. Moreover, they are utilizing both sides of the roads to uniformly cultivate them. Therefore, it is predicted that the silkworm cocoon harvest in the spring of next year will increase by three or four tenths compared to this year. It is now determined that there will be no more concerns about shortages.

Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau to Proceed with Rural Loans

The Ministry of Finance, in order to revive the rural economy, ordered all banks to allocate one-fifth of their savings deposits for agricultural loans. In addition to forming the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, which is dedicated to this purpose, all banks have established agricultural loan programs and have achieved considerable success. The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau has also received this order and is actively planning to proceed. It is reported that the principles have been decided. Previously, people were sent to Changshu and other places to investigate, intending to establish agricultural warehouse mortgage loan offices. However, due to the lack of suitable housing, they have not been established immediately. It is now known that these can be established gradually around January next year.

Outgoing Japanese Consul in Shanghai, Terasaki, Returned to His Country Last Night

Japanese Consul in Shanghai, Terasaki, was transferred back to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Last night, he took his family on the Japanese mail ship Tatsuta Maru and set off to return to his country. Colleagues including Japanese Consul General Wakasugi and Japanese expatriates went to the ship to see him off. The ship was scheduled to leave Shanghai at 7:00 am this morning. His successor, Kazaki Ichiro, arrived in Shanghai on the 30th of last month to take up his post.

Since the previous Japanese Consul General in Shanghai, Ishisha, was promoted to Ambassador to Siam, it was previously announced that the former Consul General in Guangzhou, Kawai Tatsuo, would succeed him. However, at that time, Kawai was suffering from typhoid fever and returned to his country for treatment. Temporarily, the position was concurrently held by Counselor Wakasugi of the embassy. It is now known that Kawai has recovered and is scheduled to take the Shanghai Maru from Kobe on the 18th to come to China to take up his new post, and will arrive in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 20th. Wakasugi will relinquish his position as Consul General in Shanghai after Kawai arrives in Shanghai and will devote himself to his role as Embassy Counselor.

Appeal of the Japanese Sailor Hideo Nakayama Case: Full Text of the Yang Ye Judgment (Continued)

Regarding the appellants' grounds for appeal, totaling five points, except for the third point concerning the motive for the murder, the fourth point concerning the defendant's counter-evidence, and the fifth point concerning the true facts that can be inferred from the evidence in this case, which are all speculative and ideal words and lack concrete evidence to prove them, their first argument contains many criticisms of the evidence presented by the police. Among the important points, they state that the bullet entered Hideo Nakayama's head from the back and exited from the front, and should have landed in front of the sailor, not eight feet away behind him. This court examined the original trial's sketch map, where the location where Hideo Nakayama was shot (red dot) and the place where he fell are three large steps apart. The bullet landed in the middle of these two locations (green dot), with the bullet's landing point originally in front of the location where Hideo Nakayama was shot. Furthermore, according to the diagnosis in the report of Japanese military doctor Kogawa, when Hideo Nakayama was sent to the Japanese Marine Corps headquarters after being injured, his body temperature was 36.5 degrees, his pulse was 90, and his respiration rate was 22, which were not different from those of a normal person. Therefore, it was possible for him to continue walking forward after being injured, which is self-evident. Considering that Hideo Nakayama was physically strong, it is normal for him to continue walking three steps forward before falling to the ground after suddenly being attacked. It is impossible to disregard the sketch map and insist on the theory that the bullet landed behind him, based solely on the location where he fell. Furthermore, the fact that a gun fired through an animal may not leave bloodstains, and that the bullet was fired from the gun presented in the case has been identified by experts from the Forensic Medical Research Institute and the Shanghai Municipal Council's Ordnance Department, which cannot be refuted by the appellants' empty words. Moreover, witness Zhang Chen testified that Zeng Yuan and Zheng Weimin used a pencil to draw the shape of a gun while smoking opium, and later Zeng Yuan introduced Zhang Chen to Zheng Weimin, who said that if you report to the Japanese military headquarters that Hideo Nakayama was shot by Ye Haisheng, Yang Wendao, and the Korean Jie Ke, you could get a reward of four thousand yuan. The original trial, after questioning Hui Yuan about this testimony, stated that it was completely accurate. Yang Jianzhong also admitted in the original trial that he knew Zheng Weimin, gave Yang Wendao's address to Zheng, and borrowed money from Zheng. The book with the gun shape drawn on it was fabricated by Zheng and Zeng, and Yang Jianzhong planted it. This is not without basis. However, Zhang Chen was originally on good terms with Zeng Yuan and Zheng Weilong and others, and they were jointly seeking the reward. Later, due to conflicts of interest, he voluntarily reported to the law office of Ge Zhaoji, who defended Yang Wendao, and Ye drafted the statement for him, making statements in court that benefited Yang Wendao. Whether his words are credible is questionable. Even if, as the appellants say, Zheng Weimin and others did collude to accuse someone, colluding to accuse others of crimes in order to obtain a reward is different from framing someone with false evidence. According to the testimony of Zhang Chen, it can only prove that Zheng Weimin and others had the suspicion of colluding to accuse someone, but it cannot prove how Zheng Weimin framed someone with false evidence. The original trial's failure to adopt the testimonies of Zhang Chen, Zheng Weimin, Zeng Yuan, and others cannot be said to be without merit. Furthermore, according to the Forensic Medical Research Institute's identification, the fingerprints and bloodstains left in the book are not similar to Yang Wendao's fingerprints. There are two small holes on the paper on the opposite side of the gun's safety mechanism, and the edges are curled up with rust and oil stains. It is clear that the book was rusted due to oil, and the deep marks and holes in the book were not easily formed without external pressure. It is undoubtedly clear that it was temporarily pressed. The cut marks inside the holes are still new, and the two curves in the lower left of the book and the short side close to the left in the upper left are sufficient to prove that the book was temporarily created and planted. What is even more unknown is that the fingerprints left in the book, due to the small number of lines, are mostly incomplete short lines. Therefore, it cannot be proven that Yang Wendao's fingerprints also have these lines, as explained by the Forensic Medical Research Institute in the inspection report No. 100. At most, it can only be said that it cannot prove that he has these fingerprints. How can this be taken as evidence beneficial to the appellant? Iron rust is formed by the gasification of iron in the air. The location where it is placed, the humidity of the air, and whether there is oil on the surface of the gun all affect the speed of gasification. The rust alone cannot determine the date of storage. The deep marks and holes in the book are because the weight of the gun is only 600 grams, and without external pressure (such as heavy books and other items pressed on the book) or the gun shaking inside the holes of the book, it would not be sufficient to form this kind of hole. The cut marks of the gun shape in the book are located in the middle of the book, which is not easily exposed to external light and dust, and it is difficult to determine the age of the marks. All of these were explained separately by the Forensic Medical Research Institute in the inspection report No. 99, which is on file. If the place where the gun is placed is dry and the surface is covered with oil, the gasification process can be slowed down. Since the gun has been tested for oil, which has a rust-proof effect, the appellant's claim that it caused rust, turning slowness into speed, clearly contradicts the meaning of the Forensic Medical Research Institute's identification. As for the holes in the book, they can also be caused by the gun shaking in the book and are not absolutely dependent on external pressure. How can the appellant take things out of context to use as material for attacking the original judgment? Turning to the second point of the appellant's argument, it is nothing more than that Ye Haisheng's confession and performance in the original trial were not free. This court examined the original trial records. Although Ye Haisheng's confession was not entirely consistent before and after, it was not the result of torture and was consistent with the facts, as mentioned earlier. When the judge appointed by the original trial took Ye Haisheng and witness Hu Xianghe to the site for on-site inspection, Ye Haisheng's performance on that day, as recorded in the on-site inspection record, did not involve coercion, threats, inducements, fraud, or other improper methods that would make his performance unfree. The appellant's defense lawyers also participated and acknowledged that the record was accurate, and signed it accordingly, without Ye Haisheng making any statements that his performance was not free. How can the appellant make this claim only after the appeal? Although Ye Haisheng's hands were cuffed during the on-site inspection, and he was escorted by Japanese police officers, this was merely a security measure and cannot be taken as evidence that he was not free. Furthermore, the distance between the place where Ye Haisheng demonstrated that he fired the gun and the place where Hideo Nakayama stood was five or six normal steps away, which does not match the five centimeters or so shooting distance based on the gunpowder smoke marks on Hideo Nakayama's wound, as determined by the Forensic Medical Research Institute. However, during the act of killing, his mind was disordered and he was in a state of panic. The distance from which he fired the gun was something he could not have paid attention to, so it is impossible to have a detailed memory of every inch. Therefore, the fact that there were slight discrepancies in the location where he demonstrated that he fired the gun cannot be used to completely negate the fact that he confessed to the crime. As for the testimony of witness Pan Qiaoying, who said that she saw a sailor and another person walking in the same direction, separated in the east, west, front, and back, which is not completely inconsistent with Ye Haisheng's statement that he followed behind. During the on-site inspection, the details of witness Hu Xianghe's statement that Ye Haisheng ran out from beside the pole and that the clothes of the person who ran away seemed to be those of a sailor were explained separately in the original trial's judgment, which held that the observations were mistaken. In addition, witnesses Zhu Senfu and Ji A'gen stated in the original trial that Yang Wendao of the Tongyi Association did not come often, only once or twice, and that they had not seen Haisheng and the Korean, which is inconsistent with Yang Wendao's statement that he went to the association every day to work, and with the statement of Hong Wenwei, who voluntarily surrendered to the court and testified that Yang Wendao was often at the association. Hong Wenwei stated that on the afternoon of November 9th of last year, from 7:00 PM to 11:00 PM, he was at the association with Yang Wendao. After I returned home, my child told me that a Japanese sailor had been killed, and I told Yang Wendao the next day, which also differs from Yang Wendao's statement that he only knew about it from the newspaper three or four days after the incident. This testimony is even more worthless.

In conclusion, except for the part concerning Zhou Sherong, which has already been decided and is not subject to discussion, the original trial held that the appellants' murder of Japanese sailor Hideo Nakayama was sufficient to cause disputes between China and foreign countries, and considered that the harm caused by the crime was extremely serious. Ye Haisheng was the principal offender, and Yang Wendao was the one who initiated the idea and was in a commanding position. Their circumstances are all unforgivable. According to Article 28, Paragraph 1 of Article 271, Paragraph 1 of Article 37, and Paragraph 1, Items 1 and 2 of Article 38 of the Criminal Law, they were each sentenced to death and deprived of their civil rights for life. The pistol, six bullets, one bullet casing, one bullet, and the book "Practical Physics" containing the hidden gun were ordered to be confiscated. This is not inappropriate. The appellants' arguments in support of their appeal are difficult to recognize as reasonable. According to Article 360 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the judgment should be as stated in the main text.

In this case, Prosecutor Lin Wopeng of this court attended the hearing and presented his opinions.

December 9, the 25th year of the Republic of China, Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, Presiding Judge Yu Hua, Judge Zhou Han, Judge Zhongyi, A true copy certifies that it is identical to the original.

Detectives from the French Concession police station, acting on a tip-off received around 10 p.m. the previous evening, raided a gambling den located on the second floor of 426 Fa Da Ma Road. Victim Encounters Robbers in Amusement Park: Stolen Check Cashed After Being Forced to Sign

Qian Futang, a government official from Shaoxing, Zhejiang Province, resides at No. 26, Lane 150, Shanhai Guan Road. On the morning of October 22nd of this year at 8:50 AM, three robbers from Anhui – Huang Qinghe, Tao Ziqing, and Shou Zihe – under the pretext of delivering gifts (crabs), tricked their way into the house. They barged into the room, brandishing pistols, and ordered everyone to remain silent. They forced Qian and his family into a corner and guarded them while ransacking the house for an hour. They stole jewelry and legal tender totaling 2,374 yuan. Not satisfied, the robbers knew Qian had money deposited in the Bao Yuan Qian Zhuang Bank on Tianjin Road, so they forced Qian to sign a check for 1,000 yuan on the spot. Tao Ziqing went to cash the check and returned to Qian's house. After that, they grabbed their loot and fled. Qian immediately reported the incident to the Xinzha Police Station and requested an investigation. More than a month has passed, and the case remains unsolved. Unexpectedly, Qian and his wife were at the Dajin World amusement park on Avenue Saint Marie in the French Concession the other afternoon, when they suddenly saw Huang Qinghe, one of the robbers who had robbed their house. Huang also saw Qian and his wife and tried to escape, but Qian chased and caught him, turning him over to the Annamese police, who took him to the French police station. The French police notified the Xinzha Police Station, which dispatched detective Ma Zhongrong to take Huang Qinghe back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court, where police attorney Zhang Tianyin charged him with robbery under Article 330 of the Criminal Code. He stated that the defendant confessed in the police station that he and two other fugitives, Tao Ziqing from Tongzhou and Mao Zihe (aka Lao Si) from Pudong, had robbed Qian's house. All the jewelry had been pawned at the Qiu Tianbao silver shop for 164 yuan, and the defendant had received 110 yuan. However, the defendant had previously been punished for robbery and served eight years, and the police were concerned that he might have committed other crimes within the concession, so they requested a postponement. Qian Futang submitted evidence of the robbery, and identified the defendant in court as being not only present at the scene but also the one who pretended to deliver gifts, seemingly the ringleader. Questioned by the court, the defendant admitted to the robbery. Judge Fu Lin ordered the case postponed for seven days for further questioning, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

Zhu Hong Accused of Obscenity: Luring a Young Girl Under 14 to a Hotel for Sexual Assault

Zhu Hong, 39 years old, a native of this county, residing at No. 31, Yugu Village, Yuyuan Road, was formerly the deputy director of the entertainment department at the Daxin Amusement Park. A woman from Wuxi, Shan Shen, lives at No. 241 Tianjin Road and runs a porridge shop. She has a daughter named Shan Zhenbao, currently 14 years old, studying at Qianjiang Elementary School on Ningbo Road, No. 430 Lane. Because Shan Shen has extra rooms for rent, the Metropolitan Dance Hall dancer Fan Meihua resides there, and Zhu Hong and Fan are acquaintances. In the spring of this year, Zhu visited Fan and met Zhenbao through Fan's introduction. At that time, Zhu immediately stated that he wanted to introduce Zhenbao to Daxin Amusement Park as a female employee at the billiard table, with a monthly salary of 40 or 50 yuan, up to 60 yuan. On June 2nd, Zhu invited Zhenbao to the Metropolitan Dance Hall, and after the dance, he took Zhenbao to Room 412 of the Great Eastern Hotel, using sweet words to deceive her, saying that he wanted to marry her and would give her mother several thousand yuan to buy a dowry, but she refused, saying that the matter of marriage must be approved by her mother, so there was no result. A month later, on July 7th, Shan received an invitation card from Zhu, inviting her to dinner at the Golden Dragon Restaurant. She did not suspect anything and went. However, that night, Zhu lured her to Room 308 of the Great China Hotel and forced her to have sexual intercourse. However, after achieving his goal, Zhu disappeared and never went to her place again. The girl's mother entrusted attorney Yu Xiangqin to send a letter to Zhu Hong to negotiate, but Zhu replied completely denying it. The woman reported it to the Laozha Police Station on the afternoon of the first of this month at 5:30 PM. Chinese detective Ye Yusi and Western detective No. 84 went to Zhu's house to investigate. Zhu actually believed that the detectives were impersonating police officers and illegally entered and searched, so he hired attorney Dai Ji'en to file a lawsuit against Shan Zhenbao in the Criminal Division of the First Special District Court for obstructing freedom, requesting that she be punished according to Articles 306 and 307 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Pan Zhenyang opened the Fifth Criminal Court for interrogation. Shan also hired attorney Yu Xiangqin to appear in court, and in addition to stating the circumstances of being sexually assaulted by Zhu, she also filed a counter-suit for obstructing public morals. Because Shan's birthday is the sixth day of the first lunar month, she is not yet 14 years old, so she requested that he be punished according to Paragraph 2 of Article 221 of the Criminal Law. After Judge Pan verified the confession, he ordered the case to be adjourned for investigation and interrogation.

X-ray Tuberculosis Prevention Checkup: Statistics for Last Month's Checkup: 24 Percent Healthy

The third-month checkup report for the tuberculosis prevention X-ray checkup initiated by the Chinese Tuberculosis Prevention Association Medical Committee and the Hongqiao Sanatorium is as follows: The total number of checkups was 419, including 270 men and 149 women. By occupation, there were 147 in the business world, 168 in the academic world, 10 in the education world, 15 in the industrial world, 18 civil servants, and 61 unemployed. The results of the checkup were: 101 people were completely healthy, accounting for 24 percent of the total; 52 people had active pulmonary tuberculosis, accounting for 12.3 percent of the total; 250 people had inactive pulmonary tuberculosis, accounting for 59.6 percent of the total; and 16 people had heart or aortic changes, accounting for 3.7 percent of the total. It is noteworthy that, according to statistics from previous sessions of the examination of citizens who were examined, the presence of pulmonary tuberculosis changes were all above 50 percent. Therefore, this active preventive method of early diagnosis should be deeply noted by all urban residents for preventing problems before they occur. Currently, the examination method can still purchase certificates from Shenbao first, and the location is No. A2, Daxi Road.
